claims[jwtRepo.SubjectKey]; !ok {\n   430→\t\treturn errors.New(\"lack 'sub'\")\n   431→\t} else if sub != record.User {\n   432→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"Wrong 'sub': %s\", sub)\n   433→\t}\n   434→\n   435→\tif email, ok := claims[openid.EmailKey]; !ok {\n   436→\t\treturn errors.New(\"lack 'email'\")\n   437→\t} else if email != record.Email {\n   438→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"Wrong 'email': %s\", email)\n   439→\t}\n   440→\n   441→\tnow := time.Now()\n   442→\tval, ok := claims[jwtRepo.IssuedAtKey]\n   443→\tif !ok {\n   444→\t\treturn errors.New(\"lack 'iat'\")\n   445→\t} else if iat, ok := val.(time.Time); !ok {\n   446→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"iat: %v is not a value of time.Time\", val)\n   447→\t} else if now.After(iat.Add(tokenLife)) {\n   448→\t\treturn errors.New(\"the token has been out of its life time\")\n   449→\t} else if now.Before(iat) {\n   450→\t\treturn errors.New(\"the token is issued at a future time\")\n   451→\t}\n   452→\n   453→\tif val, ok = claims[jwtRepo.ExpirationKey]; !ok {\n   454→\t\treturn errors.New(\"lack 'exp'\")\n   455→\t} else if exp, ok := val.(time.Time); !ok {\n   456→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"exp: %v is not a value of time.Time\", val)\n   457→\t} else if now.After(exp) {\n   458→\t\treturn errors.New(\"the token has been expired\")\n   459→\t}\n   460→\n   461→\t// `iss` is not required if `token_issuer` is empty in `mysql.user`\n   462→\tif iss, ok := claims[jwtRepo.IssuerKey]; ok && iss != record.AuthTokenIssuer {\n   463→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"Wrong 'iss': %s\", iss)\n   464→\t} else if !ok && len(record.AuthTokenIssuer) > 0 {\n   465→\t\treturn errors.New(\"lack 'iss'\")\n   466→\t}\n   467→\n   468→\treturn nil\n   469→}\n   470→\n   471→// CheckPasswordExpired checks whether the password has been expired.\n   472→func (*UserPrivileges) CheckPasswordExpired(sessionVars *variable.SessionVars, record *UserRecord) (bool, error) {\n   473→\tisSandBoxModeEnabled := variable.IsSandBoxModeEnabled.Load()\n   474→\tif record.PasswordExpired {\n   475→\t\tif isSandBoxModeEnabled {\n   476→\t\t\treturn true, nil\n   477→\t\t}\n   478→\t\treturn false, ErrMustChangePasswordLogin.GenWithStackByArgs()\n   479→\t}\n   480→\tif record.PasswordLifeTime != 0 {\n   481→\t\tlifeTime := record.PasswordLifeTime\n   482→\t\tif lifeTime == -1 {\n   483→\t\t\tpwdLifeTimeStr, err := sessionVars.GlobalVarsAccessor.GetGlobalSysVar(variable.DefaultPasswordLifetime)\n   484→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   485→\t\t\t\treturn false, err\n   486→\t\t\t}\n   487→\t\t\tlifeTime, err = strconv.ParseInt(pwdLifeTimeStr, 10, 64)\n   488→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   489→\t\t\t\treturn false, err\n   490→\t\t\t}\n   491→\t\t}\n   492→\t\tif lifeTime > 0 && record.PasswordLastChanged.AddDate(0, 0, int(lifeTime)).Before(time.Now()) {\n   493→\t\t\tif isSandBoxModeEnabled {\n   494→\t\t\t\treturn true, nil\n   495→\t\t\t}\n   496→\t\t\treturn false, ErrMustChangePasswordLogin.GenWithStackByArgs()\n   497→\t\t}\n   498→\t}\n   499→\treturn false, nil\n   500→}\n   501→\n   502→// GenerateAccountAutoLockErr implements the Manager interface.\n   503→func GenerateAccountAutoLockErr(failedLoginAttempts int64,\n   504→\tuser, host, lockTime, remainTime string) error {\n   505→\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(fmt.Sprintf(\"Access denied for user '%s'@'%s'.\"+\n   506→\t\t\" Account is blocked for %s day(s) (%s day(s) remaining) due to %d \"+\n   507→\t\t\"consecutive failed logins.\", user, host, lockTime,\n   508→\t\tremainTime, failedLoginAttempts))\n   509→\treturn ErUserAccessDeniedForUserAccountBlockedByPasswordLock.FastGenByArgs(user, host,\n   510→\t\tlockTime, remainTime, failedLoginAttempts)\n   511→}\n   512→\n   513→// VerifyAccountAutoLockInMemory implements the Manager interface.\n   514→func (p *UserPrivileges) VerifyAccountAutoLockInMemory(user string, host string) (bool, error) {\n   515→\tmysqlPriv := p.Handle.Get()\n   516→\trecord := mysqlPriv.matchUser(user, host)\n   517→\tif record == nil {\n   518→\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(\"get authUser privilege record fail\",\n   519→\t\t\tzap.String(\"authUser\", user), zap.String(\"authHost\", host))\n   520→\t\treturn false, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user, host)\n   521→\t}\n   522→\n   523→\tif record.AutoAccountLocked {\n   524→\t\t// If it is locked, need to check whether it can be automatically unlocked.\n   525→\t\tlockTime := record.PasswordLockTimeDays\n   526→\t\tif lockTime == -1 {\n   527→\t\t\treturn record.AutoAccountLocked, GenerateAccountAutoLockErr(record.FailedLoginAttempts, user, host, \"unlimited\", \"unlimited\")\n   528→\t\t}\n   529→\t\tlastChanged := record.AutoLockedLastChanged\n   530→\t\td := time.Now().Unix() - lastChanged\n   531→\t\tif d > lockTime*24*60*60 {\n   532→\t\t\treturn record.AutoAccountLocked, nil\n   533→\t\t}\n   534→\t\tlds := strconv.FormatInt(lockTime, 10)\n   535→\t\trds := strconv.FormatInt(int64(math.Ceil(float64(lockTime)-float64(d)/(24*60*60))), 10)\n   536→\t\treturn record.AutoAccountLocked, GenerateAccountAutoLockErr(record.FailedLoginAttempts, user, host, lds, rds)\n   537→\t}\n   538→\treturn record.AutoAccountLocked, nil\n   539→}\n   540→\n   541→// IsAccountAutoLockEnabled implements the Manager interface.\n   542→func (p *UserPrivileges) IsAccountAutoLockEnabled(user string, host string) bool {\n   543→\t// If the service is started using skip-grant-tables, the system ignores whether\n   544→\t// to enable the automatic account locking feature after continuous login failure.\n   545→\tif SkipWithGrant {\n   546→\t\tp.user = user\n   547→\t\tp.host = host\n   548→\t\treturn false\n   549→\t}\n   550→\tmysqlPriv := p.Handle.Get()\n   551→\trecord := mysqlPriv.matchUser(user, host)\n   552→\tif record == nil {\n   553→\t\treturn false\n   554→\t}\n   555→\t// For failed-login tracking and temporary locking to occur, an account's FAILED_LOGIN_ATTEMPTS\n   556→\t// and PASSWORD_LOCK_TIME options both must be nonzero.\n   557→\t// https://dev.mysql.com/doc/refman/8.0/en/create-user.html\n   558→\tif record.FailedLoginAttempts == 0 || record.PasswordLockTimeDays == 0 {\n   559→\t\treturn false\n   560→\t}\n   561→\treturn true\n   562→}\n   563→\n   564→// BuildSuccessPasswordLockingJSON builds success PasswordLocking JSON string.\n   565→func BuildSuccessPasswordLockingJSON(failedLoginAttempts, passwordLockTimeDays int64) string {\n   566→\treturn BuildPasswordLockingJSON(failedLoginAttempts, passwordLockTimeDays, \"N\", 0, time.Now().Format(time.UnixDate))\n   567→}\n   568→\n   569→// BuildPasswordLockingJSON builds PasswordLocking JSON string.\n   570→func BuildPasswordLockingJSON(failedLoginAttempts int64,\n   571→\tpasswordLockTimeDays int64, autoAccountLocked string, failedLoginCount int64, autoLockedLastChanged string) string {\n   572→\tvar passwordLockingArray []string\n   573→\tpasswordLockingArray = append(passwordLockingArray, fmt.Sprintf(\"\\\"failed_login_count\\\": %d\", failedLoginCount))\n   574→\tpasswordLockingArray = append(passwordLockingArray, fmt.Sprintf(\"\\\"failed_login_attempts\\\": %d\", failedLoginAttempts))\n   575→\tpasswordLockingArray = append(passwordLockingArray, fmt.Sprintf(\"\\\"password_lock_time_days\\\": %d\", passwordLockTimeDays))\n   576→\tif autoAccountLocked != \"\" {\n   577→\t\tpasswordLockingArray = append(passwordLockingArray, fmt.Sprintf(\"\\\"auto_account_locked\\\": \\\"%s\\\"\", autoAccountLocked))\n   578→\t}\n   579→\tif autoLockedLastChanged != \"\" {\n   580→\t\tpasswordLockingArray = fmt.Sprintf(\"{\\\"Password_locking\\\": {%s}}\", strings.Join(passwordLockingArray, \",\"))\n   584→\treturn newAttributesStr\n   585→}\n   586→\n   587→// ConnectionVerification implements the Manager interface.\n   588→func (p *UserPrivileges) ConnectionVerification(user *auth.UserIdentity, authUser, authHost string, authentication, salt []byte, sessionVars *variable.SessionVars, authConn conn.AuthConn) (info privilege.VerificationInfo, err error) {\n   589→\tif SkipWithGrant {\n   590→\t\tp.user = authUser\n   591→\t\tp.host = authHost\n   592→\t\treturn\n   593→\t}\n   594→\n 657→\t\t}\n   658→\t} else if record.AuthPlugin == mysql.AuthSocket {\n   659→\t\tif string(authentication) != authUser && string(authentication) != pwd {\n 667→\t\t\treturn info, err\n   668→\t\t}\n   669→\t} else if len(pwd) > 0 && len(authentication) > 0 {\n   670→\t\tswitch record.AuthPlugin {\n   671→\t\t// NOTE: If the checking of the clear-text 681→\t\t\t\tinfo.FailedDueToWrongPassword = true\n   682→\t\t\t\treturn info, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n   683→\t\t\t}\n   684→\t\tcase ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n   701→\t}\n   702→\n   703→\t// Login a locked account is not allowed.\n   704→\tlocked := record.AccountLocked\n   705→\tif users or root user initialized with insecure\n   711→\tif record.ResourceGroup != \"\" {\n   712→\t\tinfo.ResourceGroupName = record.ResourceGroup\n   713→\t}\n   714→\t// Skip checking password expiration if the session is migrated from another session.\n   715→\t// Otherwise, the user cannot log in or execute statements after migration.\n   716→\tif user.AuthPlugin != permission take effect.\n   723→func (p *UserPrivileges) AuthSuccess(authUser, authHost string) {\n   724→\tp.user = authUser\n   725→\tp.host = authHost\n   726→}\n   727→\n   728→type checkResult int\n   729→\n   730→const (\n   731→\tnotCheck checkResult = iota\n   732→\tpass\n   733→\tfail\n   734→)\n   735→\n   736→func (p *UserPrivileges) checkSSL(priv *globalPrivRecord, tlsState *tls.ConnectionState) bool {\n   737→\tif priv.Broken {\n   738→\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Info(\"ssl check failure, due to broken global_priv record\",\n   739→\t\t\tzap.String(\"user\", priv.User), zap.String(\"host\", priv.Host))\n   740→\t\treturn false\n   741→\t}\n   742→\tswitch priv.Priv.SSLType {\n   743→\tcase SslTypeNotSpecified, SslTypeNone:\n   744→\t\treturn true\n   745→\tcase SslTypeAny:\n   746→\t\tr := tlsState != nil\n   747→\t\tif !r {\n   748→\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Info(\"ssl check failure, require ssl but not use ssl\",\n   749→\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"user\", priv.User), zap.String(\"host\", priv.Host))\n   750→\t\t}\n   751→\t\treturn r\n   752→\tcase SslTypeX509:\n   753→\t\tif tlsState == nil {\n   754→\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Info(\"ssl check failure, require x509 but not use ssl\",\n   755→\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"user\", priv.User), zap.String(\"host\", priv.Host))\n   756→\t\t\treturn false\n   757→\t\t}\n   758→\t\thasCert := false\n   759→\t\tfor _, chain := range tlsState.VerifiedChains {\n   760→\t\t\tif len(chain) > 0 {\n   761→\t\t\t\thasCert = true\n   762→\t\t\t\tbreak\n   763→\t\t\t}\n   764→\t\t}\n   765→\t\tif !hasCert {\n   766→\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Info(\"ssl check failure, require x509 but no verified cert\",\n   767→\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"user\", priv.User), zap.String(\"host\", priv.Host))\n   768→\t\t}\n   769→\t\treturn hasCert\n   770→\tcase SslTypeSpecified:\n   771→\t\tif tlsState == nil {\n   772→\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Info(\"ssl check failure, require subject/issuer/cipher but not use ssl\",\n   773→\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"user\", priv.User), zap.String(\"host\", priv.Host))\n   774→\t\t\treturn false\n   775→\t\t}\n   776→\t\tif len(priv.Priv.SSLCipher) > 0 && priv.Priv.SSLCipher != util.TLSCipher2String(tlsState.CipherSuite) {\n   777→\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Info(\"ssl check failure for cipher\", zap.String(\"user\", priv.User), zap.String(\"host\", priv.Host),\n   778→\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"require\", priv.Priv.SSLCipher), zap.String(\"given\", util.TLSCipher2String(tlsState.CipherSuite)))\n   779→\t\t\treturn false\n   780→\t\t}\n   781→\t\tvar (\n   782→\t\t\thasCert      = false\n   783→\t\t\tmatchIssuer  checkResult\n   784→\t\t\tmatchSubject checkResult\n   785→\t\t\tmatchSAN     checkResult\n   786→\t\t)\n   787→\t\tfor _, chain := range tlsState.VerifiedChains {\n   788→\t\t\tif len(chain) == 0 {\n   789→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   790→\t\t\t}\n   791→\t\t\tcert := chain[0]\n   792→\t\t\tif len(priv.Priv.X509Issuer) > 0 {\n   793→\t\t\t\tgiven := util.X509NameOnline(cert.Issuer)\n   794→\t\t\t\tif priv.Priv.X509Issuer == given {\n   795→\t\t\t\t\tmatchIssuer = pass\n   796→\t\t\t\t} else if matchIssuer == notCheck {\n   797→\t\t\t\t\tmatchIssuer = fail\n   798→\t\t\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Info(\"ssl check failure for issuer\", zap.String(\"user\", priv.User), zap.String(\"host\", priv.Host),\n   799→\t\t\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"require\", priv.Priv.X509Issuer), zap.String(\"given\", given))\n   800→\t\t\t\t}\n   801→\t\t\t}\n   802→\t\t\tif len(priv.Priv.X509Subject) > 0 {\n   803→\t\t\t\tgiven := util.X509NameOnline(cert.Subject)\n   804→\t\t\t\tif priv.Priv.X509Subject == given {\n   805→\t\t\t\t\tmatchSubject = pass\n   806→\t\t\t\t} else if matchSubject == notCheck {\n   807→\t\t\t\t\tmatchSubject = fail\n   808→\t\t\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Info(\"ssl check failure for subject\", zap.String(\"user\", priv.User), zap.String(\"host\", priv.Host),\n   809→\t\t\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"require\", priv.Priv.X509Subject), zap.String(\"given\", given))\n   810→\t\t\t\t}\n   811→\t\t\t}\n   812→\t\t\tif len(priv.Priv.SANs) > 0 {\n   813→\t\t\t\tmatchOne := checkCertSAN(priv, cert, priv.Priv.SANs)\n   814→\t\t\t\tif matchOne {\n   815→\t\t\t\t\tmatchSAN = pass\n   816→\t\t\t\t} else if matchSAN == notCheck {\n   817→\t\t\t\t\tmatchSAN = fail\n   818→\t\t\t\t}\n   819→\t\t\t}\n   820→\t\t\thasCert = true\n   821→\t\t}\n   822→\t\tcheckResult := hasCert && matchIssuer != fail && matchSubject != fail && matchSAN != fail\n   823→\t\tif !checkResult && !hasCert {\n   824→\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Info(\"ssl check failure, require issuer/subject/SAN but no verified cert\",\n   825→\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"user\", priv.User), zap.String(\"host\", priv.Host))\n   826→\t\t}\n   827→\t\treturn checkResult\n   828→\tdefault:\n   829→\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"support ssl_type: %d\", priv.Priv.SSLType))\n   830→\t}\n   831→}\n   832→\n   833→func checkCertSAN(priv *globalPrivRecord, cert *x509.Certificate, sans map[util.SANType][]string) (r bool) {\n   834→\tr = true\n   835→\tfor typ, requireOr := range sans {\n   836→\t\tvar (\n   837→\t\t\tunsupported bool\n   838→\t\t\tgiven       []string\n   839→\t\t)\n   840→\t\tswitch typ {\n   841→\t\tcase util.URI:\n   842→\t\t\tfor _, uri := range cert.URIs {\n   843→\t\t\t\tgiven = append(given, uri.String())\n   844→\t\t\t}\n   845→\t\tcase util.DNS:\n   846→\t\t\tgiven = cert.DNSNames\n   847→\t\tcase util.IP:\n   848→\t\t\tfor _, ip := range cert.IPAddresses {\n   849→\t\t\t\tgiven = append(given, ip.String())\n   850→\t\t\t}\n   851→\t\tdefault:\n   852→\t\t\tunsupported = true\n   853→\t\t}\n   854→\t\tif unsupported {\n   855→\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Warn(\"skip unsupported SAN type\", zap.String(\"type\", string(typ)),\n   856→\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"user\", priv.User), zap.String(\"host\", priv.Host))\n   857→\t\t\tcontinue\n   858→\t\t}\n   859→\t\tvar givenMatchOne bool\n   860→\t\tfor _, req := range requireOr {\n   861→\t\t\tfor _, give := range given {\n   862→\t\t\t\tif req == give {\n authConn,\n\t}\n\tif err := authPlugin.AuthenticateUser(authRequest); err != nil {\n\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Warn(\"verify through extension auth plugin failed\",\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"plugin\", authPlugin.Name), zap.String(\"username\", user.Username), zap.Error(err))\n\t\thasPassword := \"YES\"\n\t\tif len(authentication) == 0 {\n\t\t\thasPassword = \"NO\"\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n\t}\n\n\t// If the user is authenticated using extension auth plugin, populate the plugin request verification funcs\n\tif authPlugin.VerifyPrivilege != nil {\n\t\tp.authPluginRequestVerification = func(user, host string, activeRoles []*auth.RoleIdentity, db, table, column string, priv mysql.PrivilegeType) bool {\n\t\t\treturn authPlugin.VerifyPrivilege(extension.VerifyStaticPrivRequest{\n\t\t\t\tUser:        user,\n\t\t\t\tHost:        host,\n\t\t\t\tDB:          db,\n\t\t\t\tTable:       table,\n\t\t\t\tColumn:      column,\n\t\t\t\tStaticPriv:  priv,\n\t\t\t\tConnState:   sessionVars.TLSConnectionState,\n\t\t\t\tActiveRoles: activeRoles,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif authPlugin.VerifyDynamicPrivilege != nil {\n\t\tp.authPluginRequestDynamicVerification = func(activeRoles []*auth.RoleIdentity, user, host, privName string, grantable bool) bool {\n\t\t\treturn authPlugin.VerifyDynamicPrivilege(extension.VerifyDynamicPrivRequest{\n\t\t\t\tUser:        user,\n\t\t\t\tHost:        host,\n\t\t\t\tDynamicPriv: privName,\n\t\t\t\tConnState:   sessionVars.TLSConnectionState,\n\t\t\t\tActiveRoles: activeRoles,\n\t\t\t\tWithGrant:   grantable,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc (p *UserPrivileges) isValidHash(record *UserRecord) bool {\n\tpwd := record.AuthenticationString\n\tif pwd == \"\" {\n\t\treturn true\n\t}\n\tif authPlugin, ok := p.authPlugins[record.AuthPlugin]; ok {\n\t\treturn authPlugin.ValidateAuthString(pwd)\n\t}\n\tswitch record.AuthPlugin {\n\tcase mysql.AuthNativePassword:\n\t\tif len(pwd) == mysql.PWDHashLen+1 {\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(\"the password from the mysql.user table does not match the definition of a mysql_native_password\", zap.String(\"user\", record.User), zap.String(\"plugin\", record.AuthPlugin), zap.Int(\"hash_length\", len(pwd)))\n\t\treturn false\n\tcase mysql.AuthCachingSha2Password:\n\t\tif len(pwd) == mysql.SHAPWDHashLen {\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(\"the password from the mysql.user table does not match the definition of a caching_sha2_password\", zap.String(\"user\", record.User), zap.String(\"plugin\", record.AuthPlugin), zap.Int(\"hash_length\", len(pwd)))\n\t\treturn false\n\tcase mysql.AuthTiDBSM3Password:\n\t\tif len(pwd) == mysql.SM3PWDHashLen {\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(\"the password from the mysql.user table does not match the definition of a tidb_sm3_password\", zap.String(\"user\", record.User), zap.String(\"plugin\", record.AuthPlugin), zap.Int(\"hash_length\", len(pwd)))\n\t\treturn false\n\tcase mysql.AuthSocket:\n\t\treturn true\n\tcase mysql.AuthTiDBAuthToken:\n\t\treturn true\n\tcase mysql.AuthLDAPSimple, mysql.AuthLDAPSASL:\n\t\treturn true\n\t}\n\n\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(\"user password from the mysql.user table not like a known hash format\", zap.String(\"user\", record.User), zap.String(\"plugin\", record.AuthPlugin), zap.Int(\"hash_length\", len(pwd)))\n\treturn false\n}\n\n// GetEncodedPassword implements the Manager interface.\nfunc (p *UserPrivileges) GetEncodedPassword(user, host string) string {\n\tmysqlPriv := p.Handle.Get()\n\trecord := mysqlPriv.connectionVerification(user, host)\n\tif record == nil {\n\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(\"get user privilege record fail\",\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"user\", user), zap.String(\"host\", host))\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\tif p.isValidHash(record) {\n\t\treturn record.AuthenticationString\n\t}\n\treturn \"\"\n}\n\n// GetAuthPluginForConnection gets the authentication plugin used in connection establishment.\nfunc (p *UserPrivileges) GetAuthPluginForConnection(user, host string) (string, error) {\n\tif SkipWithGrant {\n\t\treturn mysql.AuthNativePassword, nil\n\t}\n\n\tmysqlPriv := p.Handle.Get()\n\trecord := mysqlPriv.connectionVerification(user, host)\n\tif record == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\", errors.New(\"Failed to get user record\")\n\t}\n\tif authPlugin, ok := p.authPlugins[record.AuthPlugin]; ok {\n\t\treturn authPlugin.Name, nil\n\t}\n\tswitch record.AuthPlugin {\n\tcase mysql.AuthTiDBAuthToken, mysql.AuthLDAPSASL, mysql.AuthLDAPSimple:\n\t\treturn record.AuthPlugin, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// zero-length auth string means no password for native and caching_sha2 auth.\n\t// but for auth_socket it means there should be a 1-to-1 mapping between the TiDB user\n\t// and the OS user.\n\tif record.AuthenticationString == \"\" && record.AuthPlugin != mysql.AuthSocket {\n\t\treturn \"\", nil\n\t}\n\tif p.isValidHash(record) {\n\t\treturn record.AuthPlugin, nil\n\t}\n\treturn \"\", errors.New(\"Failed to get plugin for user\")\n}\n\n// GetAuthPlugin gets the authentication plugin for the account identified by the user and host\nfunc (p *UserPrivileges) GetAuthPlugin(user, host string) (string, error) {\n\tif SkipWithGrant {\n\t\treturn mysql.AuthNativePassword, nil\n\t}\n\tmysqlPriv := p.Handle.Get()\n\trecord := mysqlPriv.connectionVerification(user, host)\n\tif record == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\", errors.New(\"Failed to get user record\")\n\t}\n\tif !p.isValidHash(record) {\n\t\treturn \"\", errors.New(\"Failed to get plugin for user\")\n\t}\n\treturn record.AuthPlugin, nil\n}\n\n// MatchIdentity implements the Manager interface.\nfunc (p *UserPrivileges) MatchIdentity(user, host string, skipNameResolve bool) (u string, h string, success bool) {\n\tif SkipWithGrant {\n\t\treturn user, host, true\n\t}\n\tif err := p.Handle.ensureActiveUser(user); err != nil {\n\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(\"ensure user data fail\",\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"user\", user))\n\t}\n\tmysqlPriv := p.Handle.Get()\n\trecord := mysqlPriv.matchIdentity(p.Handle.sctx, user, host, skipNameResolve)\n\tif record != nil {\n\t\treturn record.User, record.Host, true\n\t}\n\treturn \"\", \"\", false\n}\n\n// MatchUserResourceGroupName implements the Manager interface.\nfunc (p *UserPrivileges) MatchUserResourceGroupName(resourceGroupName string) (u string, success bool) {\n\tmysqlPriv := p.Handle.Get()\n\trecord := mysqlPriv.matchResoureGroup(resourceGroupName)\n\tif record != nil {\n\t\treturn record.User, true\n\t}\n\treturn \"\", false\n}\n\n// GetAuthWithoutVerification implements the Manager interface.\nfunc (p *UserPrivileges) GetAuthWithoutVerification(user, host string) (success bool) {\n\tif SkipWithGrant {\n\t\tp.user = user\n\t\tp.host = host\n\t\tsuccess = true\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tmysqlPriv := p.Handle.Get()\n\trecord := mysqlPriv.connectionVerification(user, host)\n\tif record == nil {\n\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(\"get user privilege record fail\",\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"user\", user), zap.String(\"host\", host))\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tp.user = user\n\tp.host = record.Host\n\tsuccess = true\n\treturn\n}\n\nfunc checkAuthTokenClaims(claims map[string]any, record *UserRecord, tokenLife time.Duration) error {\n\tif sub, ok := claims[jwtRepo.SubjectKey]; !ok {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"lack 'sub'\")\n\t} else if sub != record.User {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"Wrong 'sub': %s\", sub)\n\t}\n\n\tif email, ok := claims[openid.EmailKey]; !ok {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"lack 'email'\")\n\t} else if email != record.Email {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"Wrong 'email': %s\", email)\n\t}\n\n\tnow := time.Now()\n\tval, ok := claims[jwtRepo.IssuedAtKey]\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"lack 'iat'\")\n\t} else if iat, ok := val.(time.Time); !ok {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"iat: %v is not a value of time.Time\", val)\n\t} else if now.After(iat.Add(tokenLife)) {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"the token has been out of its life time\")\n\t} else if now.Before(iat) {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"the token is issued at a future time\")\n\t}\n\n\tif val, ok = claims[jwtRepo.ExpirationKey]; !ok {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"lack 'exp'\")\n\t} else if exp, ok := val.(time.Time); !ok {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"exp: %v is not a value of time.Time\", val)\n\t} else if now.After(exp) {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"the token has been expired\")\n\t}\n\n\t// `iss` is not required if `token_issuer` is empty in `mysql.user`\n\tif iss, ok := claims[jwtRepo.IssuerKey]; ok && iss != record.AuthTokenIssuer {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"Wrong 'iss': %s\", iss)\n\t} else if !ok && len(record.AuthTokenIssuer) > 0 {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"lack 'iss'\")\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// CheckPasswordExpired checks whether the password has been expired.\nfunc (*UserPrivileges) CheckPasswordExpired(sessionVars *variable.SessionVars, record *UserRecord) (bool, error) {\n\tisSandBoxModeEnabled := variable.IsSandBoxModeEnabled.Load()\n\tif record.PasswordExpired {\n\t\tif isSandBoxModeEnabled {\n\t\t\treturn true, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn false, ErrMustChangePasswordLogin.GenWithStackByArgs()\n\t}\n\tif record.PasswordLifeTime != 0 {\n\t\tlifeTime := record.PasswordLifeTime\n\t\tif lifeTime == -1 {\n\t\t\tpwdLifeTimeStr, err := sessionVars.GlobalVarsAccessor.GetGlobalSysVar(variable.DefaultPasswordLifetime)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn false, err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tlifeTime, err = strconv.ParseInt(pwdLifeTimeStr, 10, 64)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn false, err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\tif lifeTime > 0 && record.PasswordLastChanged.AddDate(0, 0, int(lifeTime)).Before(time.Now()) {\n\t\t\tif isSandBoxModeEnabled {\n\t\t\t\treturn true, nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn false, ErrMustChangePasswordLogin.GenWithStackByArgs()\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn false, nil\n}\n\n// GenerateAccountAutoLockErr implements the Manager interface.\nfunc GenerateAccountAutoLockErr(failedLoginAttempts int64,\n\tuser, host, lockTime, remainTime string) error {\n\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(fmt.Sprintf(\"Access denied for user '%s'@'%s'.\"+\n\t\t\" Account is blocked for %s day(s) (%s day(s) remaining) due to %d \"+\n\t\t\"consecutive failed logins.\", user, host, lockTime,\n\t\tremainTime, failedLoginAttempts))\n\treturn ErUserAccessDeniedForUserAccountBlockedByPasswordLock.FastGenByArgs(user, host,\n\t\tlockTime, remainTime, failedLoginAttempts)\n}\n\n// VerifyAccountAutoLockInMemory implements the Manager interface.\nfunc (p *UserPrivileges) VerifyAccountAutoLockInMemory(user string, host string) (bool, error) {\n\tmysqlPriv := p.Handle.Get()\n\trecord := mysqlPriv.matchUser(user, host)\n\tif record == nil {\n\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(\"get authUser privilege record fail\",\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"authUser\", user), zap.String(\"authHost\", host))\n\t\treturn false, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user, host)\n\t}\n\n\tif record.AutoAccountLocked {\n\t\t// If it is locked, need to check whether it can be automatically unlocked.\n\t\tlockTime := record.PasswordLockTimeDays\n\t\tif lockTime == -1 {\n\t\t\treturn record.AutoAccountLocked, GenerateAccountAutoLockErr(record.FailedLoginAttempts, user, host, \"unlimited\", \"unlimited\")\n\t\t}\n\t\tlastChanged := record.AutoLockedLastChanged\n\t\td := time.Now().Unix() - lastChanged\n\t\tif d > lockTime*24*60*60 {\n\t\t\treturn record.AutoAccountLocked, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tlds := strconv.FormatInt(lockTime, 10)\n\t\trds := strconv.FormatInt(int64(math.Ceil(float64(lockTime)-float64(d)/(24*60*60))), 10)\n\t\treturn record.AutoAccountLocked, GenerateAccountAutoLockErr(record.FailedLoginAttempts, user, host, lds, rds)\n\t}\n\treturn record.AutoAccountLocked, nil\n}\n\n// IsAccountAutoLockEnabled implements the Manager interface.\nfunc (p *UserPrivileges) IsAccountAutoLockEnabled(user string, host string) bool {\n\t// If the service is started using skip-grant-tables, the system ignores whether\n\t// to enable the automatic account locking feature after continuous login failure.\n\tif SkipWithGrant {\n\t\tp.user = user\n\t\tp.host = host\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\tmysqlPriv := p.Handle.Get()\n\trecord := mysqlPriv.matchUser(user, host)\n\tif record == nil {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\t// For failed-login tracking and temporary locking to occur, an account's FAILED_LOGIN_ATTEMPTS\n\t// and PASSWORD_LOCK_TIME options both must be nonzero.\n\t// https://dev.mysql.com/doc/refman/8.0/en/create-user.html\n\tif record.FailedLoginAttempts == 0 || record.PasswordLockTimeDays == 0 {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\treturn true\n}\n\n// BuildSuccessPasswordLockingJSON builds success PasswordLocking JSON string.\nfunc BuildSuccessPasswordLockingJSON(failedLoginAttempts, passwordLockTimeDays int64) string {\n\treturn BuildPasswordLockingJSON(failedLoginAttempts, passwordLockTimeDays, \"N\", 0, time.Now().Format(time.UnixDate))\n}\n\n// BuildPasswordLockingJSON builds PasswordLocking JSON string.\nfunc BuildPasswordLockingJSON(failedLoginAttempts int64,\n\tpasswordLockTimeDays int64, autoAccountLocked string, failedLoginCount int64, autoLockedLastChanged string) string {\n\tvar passwordLockingArray []string\n\tpasswordLockingArray = append(passwordLockingArray, fmt.Sprintf(\"\\\"failed_login_count\\\": %d\", failedLoginCount))\n\tpasswordLockingArray = append(passwordLockingArray, fmt.Sprintf(\"\\\"failed_login_attempts\\\": %d\", failedLoginAttempts))\n\tpasswordLockingArray = append(passwordLockingArray, fmt.Sprintf(\"\\\"password_lock_time_days\\\": %d\", passwordLockTimeDays))\n\tif autoAccountLocked != \"\" {\n\t\tpasswordLockingArray = append(passwordLockingArray, fmt.Sprintf(\"\\\"auto_account_locked\\\": \\\"%s\\\"\", autoAccountLocked))\n\t}\n\tif autoLockedLastChanged != \"\" {\n\t\tpasswordLockingArray = append(passwordLockingArray, fmt.Sprintf(\"\\\"auto_locked_last_changed\\\": \\\"%s\\\"\", autoLockedLastChanged))\n\t}\n\n\tnewAttributesStr := fmt.Sprintf(\"{\\\"Password_locking\\\": {%s}}\", strings.Join(passwordLockingArray, \",\"))\n\treturn newAttributesStr\n}\n\n// ConnectionVerification implements the Manager interface.\nfunc (p *UserPrivileges) ConnectionVerification(user *auth.UserIdentity, authUser, authHost string, authentication, salt []byte, sessionVars *variable.SessionVars, authConn conn.AuthConn) (info privilege.VerificationInfo, err error) {\n\tif SkipWithGrant {\n\t\tp.user = authUser\n\t\tp.host = authHost\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\thasPassword := \"YES\"\n\tif len(authentication) == 0 {\n\t\thasPassword = \"NO\"\n\t}\n\n\tmysqlPriv := p.Handle.Get()\n\trecord := mysqlPriv.connectionVerification(authUser, authHost)\n\n\tif record == nil {\n\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(\"get authUser privilege record fail\",\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"authUser\", authUser), zap.String(\"authHost\", authHost))\n\t\treturn info, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n\t}\n\n\tglobalPriv := mysqlPriv.matchGlobalPriv(authUser, authHost)\n\tif globalPriv != nil {\n\t\tif !p.checkSSL(globalPriv, sessionVars.TLSConnectionState) {\n\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(\"global priv check ssl fail\",\n\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"authUser\", authUser), zap.String(\"authHost\", authHost))\n\t\t\treturn info, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tpwd := record.AuthenticationString\n\tif !p.isValidHash(record) {\n\t\treturn info, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n\t}\n\n\t// If the user uses session token to log in, skip checking record.AuthPlugin.\n\tif user.AuthPlugin == mysql.AuthTiDBSessionToken {\n\t\tif err = sessionstates.ValidateSessionToken(authentication, user.Username); err != nil {\n\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Warn(\"verify session token failed\", zap.String(\"username\", user.Username), zap.Error(err))\n\t\t\treturn info, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n\t\t}\n\t} else if record.AuthPlugin == mysql.AuthTiDBAuthToken {\n\t\tif len(authentication) == 0 {\n\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(\"empty authentication\")\n\t\t\treturn info, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n\t\t}\n\t\ttokenString := string(hack.String(authentication[:len(authentication)-1]))\n\t\tvar (\n\t\t\tclaims map[string]any\n\t\t)\n\t\tif claims, err = GlobalJWKS.checkSigWithRetry(tokenString, 1); err != nil {\n\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(\"verify JWT failed\", zap.Error(err))\n\t\t\treturn info, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n\t\t}\n\t\tif err = checkAuthTokenClaims(claims, record, defaultTokenLife); err != nil {\n\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(\"check claims failed\", zap.Error(err))\n\t\t\treturn info, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n\t\t}\n\t} else if record.AuthPlugin == mysql.AuthLDAPSASL {\n\t\tif err = ldap.LDAPSASLAuthImpl.AuthLDAPSASL(authUser, pwd, authentication, authConn); err != nil {\n\t\t\t// though the pwd stores only `dn` for LDAP SASL, it could be unsafe to print it out.\n\t\t\t// for example, someone may alter the auth plugin name but forgot to change the password...\n\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Warn(\"verify through LDAP SASL failed\", zap.String(\"username\", user.Username), zap.Error(err))\n\t\t\treturn info, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n\t\t}\n\t} else if record.AuthPlugin == mysql.AuthLDAPSimple {\n\t\tif err = ldap.LDAPSimpleAuthImpl.AuthLDAPSimple(authUser, pwd, authentication); err != nil {\n\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Warn(\"verify through LDAP Simple failed\", zap.String(\"username\", user.Username), zap.Error(err))\n\t\t\treturn info, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n\t\t}\n\t} else if record.AuthPlugin == mysql.AuthSocket {\n\t\tif string(authentication) != authUser && string(authentication) != pwd {\n\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(\"Failed socket auth\", zap.String(\"authUser\", authUser),\n\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"socket_user\", string(authentication)),\n\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"authentication_string\", pwd))\n\t\t\treturn info, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n\t\t}\n\t} else if authPlugin, ok := p.authPlugins[record.AuthPlugin]; ok {\n\t\tif err = p.authenticateWithPlugin(user, authentication, salt, sessionVars, authConn, authPlugin, pwd); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn info, err\n\t\t}\n\t} else if len(pwd) > 0 && len(authentication) > 0 {\n\t\tswitch record.AuthPlugin {\n\t\t// NOTE: If the checking of the clear-text password fails, please set `info.FailedDueToWrongPassword = true`.\n\t\tcase mysql.AuthNativePassword:\n\t\t\thpwd, err := auth.DecodePassword(pwd)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(\"decode password string failed\", zap.Error(err))\n\t\t\t\tinfo.FailedDueToWrongPassword = true\n\t\t\t\treturn info, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif !auth.CheckScrambledPassword(salt, hpwd, authentication) {\n\t\t\t\tinfo.FailedDueToWrongPassword = true\n\t\t\t\treturn info, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\tcase mysql.AuthCachingSha2Password, mysql.AuthTiDBSM3Password:\n\t\t\tauthok, err := auth.CheckHashingPassword([]byte(pwd), string(authentication), record.AuthPlugin)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(\"Failed to check caching_sha2_password\", zap.Error(err))\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif !authok {\n\t\t\t\tinfo.FailedDueToWrongPassword = true\n\t\t\t\treturn info, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(\"unknown authentication plugin\", zap.String(\"authUser\", authUser), zap.String(\"plugin\", record.AuthPlugin))\n\t\t\treturn info, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n\t\t}\n\t} else if len(pwd) > 0 || len(authentication) > 0 {\n\t\tinfo.FailedDueToWrongPassword = true\n\t\treturn info, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n\t}\n\n\t// Login a locked account is not allowed.\n\tlocked := record.AccountLocked\n\tif locked {\n\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(fmt.Sprintf(\"Access denied for authUser '%s'@'%s'. Account is locked.\", authUser, authHost))\n\t\treturn info, errAccountHasBeenLocked.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname)\n\t}\n\n\t// special handling to existing users or root user initialized with insecure\n\tif record.ResourceGroup != \"\" {\n\t\tinfo.ResourceGroupName = record.ResourceGroup\n\t}\n\t// Skip checking password expiration if the session is migrated from another session.\n\t// Otherwise, the user cannot log in or execute statements after migration.\n\tif user.AuthPlugin != mysql.AuthTiDBSessionToken {\n\t\tinfo.InSandBoxMode, err = p.CheckPasswordExpired(sessionVars, record)\n\t}\n\treturn\n}\n\n// AuthSuccess is to make the permission take effect.\nfunc (p *UserPrivileges) AuthSuccess(authUser, authHost string) {\n\tp.user = authUser\n\tp.host = authHost\n}\n\ntype checkResult int\n\nconst (\n\tnotCheck checkResult = iota\n\tpass\n\tfail\n)\n\nfunc (p *UserPrivileges) checkSSL(priv *globalPrivRecord, tlsState *tls.ConnectionState) bool {\n\tif priv.Broken {\n\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Info(\"ssl check failure, due to broken global_priv record\",\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"user\", priv.User), zap.String(\"host\", priv.Host))\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\tswitch priv.Priv.SSLType {\n\tcase SslTypeNotSpecified, SslTypeNone:\n\t\treturn true\n\tcase SslTypeAny:\n\t\tr := tlsState != nil\n\t\tif !r {\n\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Info(\"ssl check failure, require ssl but not use ssl\",\n\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"user\", priv.User), zap.String(\"host\", priv.Host))\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn r\n\tcase SslTypeX509:\n\t\tif tlsState == nil {\n\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Info(\"ssl check failure, require x509 but not use ssl\",\n\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"user\", priv.User), zap.String(\"host\", priv.Host))\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\t\thasCert := false\n\t\tfor _, chain := range tlsState.VerifiedChains {\n\t\t\tif len(chain) > 0 {\n\t\t\t\thasCert = true\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\tif !hasCert {\n\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Info(\"ssl check failure, require x509 but no verified cert\",\n\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"user\", priv.User), pkg/privilege/ and pkg/planner/.\\n\\n## PrivilegeManager Interface\\n\\n`pkg/privilege/privilege.go` defines the `Manager` interface — the central contract for all privilege operations. Key methods include `RequestVerification(activeRole, db, table, column, priv)` for static privilege checks, `RequestDynamicVerification(activeRoles, privName, grantable)` for dynamic privileges (BACKUP_ADMIN, ROLE_ADMIN, etc.), `ConnectionVerification` for login auth, `ShowGrants`, `ActiveRoles`, `FindEdge`, `GetDefaultRoles`, and `GetAllRoles`. `GetPrivilegeManager` retrieves the bound Manager from the session context; `BindPrivilegeManager` sets it.\\n\\n## UserPrivileges (Manager implementation)\\n\\n`pkg/privilege/privileges/privileges.go` contains `UserPrivileges`, the concrete implementation of `privilege.Manager`. Its `RequestVerification` method: (1) handles SkipWithGrant bypass; (2) enforces SEM (Security Enhanced Mode) hard rules via `RequestDynamicVerification`; (3) invokes extension access-check hooks; (4) delegates to `MySQLPrivilege.RequestVerification` from the cache; (5) optionally calls an auth-plugin-specific verification function. `RequestDynamicVerification` similarly delegates to `MySQLPrivilege.RequestDynamicVerification`, which falls back to SUPER privilege for compatibility.\\n\\n## MySQLPrivilege Cache\\n\\n`pkg/privilege/privileges/cache.go` is the largest and most critical file. It defines:\\n- `MySQLPrivilege` struct: the in-memory cache of all MySQL privilege tables (mysql.user, mysql.db, mysql.tables_priv, mysql.columns_priv, mysql.global_priv, mysql.global_grants, mysql.role_edges, mysql.default_roles). It is populated by `LoadAll` which issues SQL queries defined as constants (sqlLoadUserTable, sqlLoadDBTable, sqlLoadTablePrivTable, etc.).\\n- `Handle` struct (line 1818): wraps a `*MySQLPrivilege` and provides `Get()` to retrieve the current snapshot and `Update()` to reload.\\n- `roleGraphEdgesTable` (line 248): per-user map of role edges loaded from mysql.role_edges.\\n- `roleGraph map[string]roleGraphEdgesTable` (line 275): the adjacency list of the role inheritance graph.\\n- `LoadRoleGraph` (line 541): populates `roleGraph` from mysql.role_edges.\\n- `FindRole` (line 340): checks if a direct edge exists between a user and role.\\n- `FindAllRole` (line 315): BFS traversal of `roleGraph` to expand all transitively reachable roles from a set of active roles.\\n- `FindAllUserEffectiveRoles` (line 304): filters `activeRoles` against granted roles for the user, then calls `FindAllRole` to do full BFS expansion — this is the core role graph resolution used before every privilege check.\\n- `RequestVerification` (line 1333): calls `FindAllUserEffectiveRoles` to get the full role list, then checks user-level, db-level, table-level, and column-level privileges in order, OR-ing the privilege bitmask across all roles.\\n- `RequestDynamicVerification` (line 1311): calls `HasExplicitlyGrantedDynamicPrivilege`, then falls back to SUPER if SEM permits.\\n- `HasExplicitlyGrantedDynamicPrivilege` (line 1287): checks mysql.global_grants for the dynamic privilege, looping over all effective roles.\\n\\n## SQL Statement → Required Privileges Mapping\\n\\n`pkg/planner/core/planbuilder.go` defines the `visitInfo` struct (line 81) — the data structure recording what privilege is required for which db/table/column. Functions `appendVisitInfo` and `appendDynamicVisitInfo` (defined in `pkg/planner/core/logical_plan_builder.go`) populate the builder's `visitInfo` slice as each SQL clause is processed. `planbuilder.go` contains the main `Build` method dispatch and handles DDL statements (CREATE/DROP/ALTER TABLE, GRANT, REVOKE, SHOW, ADMIN, SET, KILL, etc.), mapping each to specific `mysql.XxxPriv` constants or dynamic privilege names. For example: SHOW CREATE TABLE → ShowViewPriv; SHOW PROCESSLIST → ProcessPriv; SET GLOBAL → SYSTEM_VARIABLES_ADMIN dynamic; KILL → CONNECTION_ADMIN dynamic; GRANT/REVOKE → GrantPriv + SuperPriv or dynamic.\\n\\n`pkg/planner/core/logical_plan_builder.go` handles DML: SELECT → SelectPriv, INSERT → InsertPriv, UPDATE → UpdatePriv, DELETE → DeletePriv. It also checks view definer privileges via `RequestVerificationWithUser` (line 5016) to enforce SQL SECURITY DEFINER semantics.\\n\\n## CheckPrivilege and Its pkg/privilege/ and pkg/planner/.\\n\\n## PrivilegeManager Interface\\n\\n`pkg/privilege/privilege.go` defines the `Manager` interface — the central contract for all privilege operations. Key methods include `RequestVerification(activeRole, db, table, column, priv)` for static privilege checks, `RequestDynamicVerification(activeRoles, privName, grantable)` for dynamic privileges (BACKUP_ADMIN, ROLE_ADMIN, etc.), `ConnectionVerification` for login auth, `ShowGrants`, `ActiveRoles`, `FindEdge`, `GetDefaultRoles`, and `GetAllRoles`. `GetPrivilegeManager` retrieves the bound Manager from the session context; `BindPrivilegeManager` sets it.\\n\\n## UserPrivileges (Manager implementation)\\n\\n`pkg/privilege/privileges/privileges.go` contains `UserPrivileges`, the concrete implementation of `privilege.Manager`. Its `RequestVerification` method: (1) handles SkipWithGrant bypass; (2) enforces SEM (Security Enhanced Mode) hard rules via `RequestDynamicVerification`; (3) invokes extension access-check hooks; (4) delegates to `MySQLPrivilege.RequestVerification` from the cache; (5) optionally calls an auth-plugin-specific verification function. `RequestDynamicVerification` similarly delegates to `MySQLPrivilege.RequestDynamicVerification`, which falls back to SUPER privilege for compatibility.\\n\\n## MySQLPrivilege Cache\\n\\n`pkg/privilege/privileges/cache.go` is the largest and most critical file. It defines:\\n- `MySQLPrivilege` struct: the in-memory cache of all MySQL privilege tables (mysql.user, mysql.db, mysql.tables_priv, mysql.columns_priv, mysql.global_priv, mysql.global_grants, mysql.role_edges, mysql.default_roles). It is populated by `LoadAll` which issues SQL queries defined as constants (sqlLoadUserTable, sqlLoadDBTable, sqlLoadTablePrivTable, etc.).\\n- `Handle` struct (line 1818): wraps a `*MySQLPrivilege` and provides `Get()` to retrieve the current snapshot and `Update()` to reload.\\n- `roleGraphEdgesTable` (line 248): per-user map of role edges loaded from mysql.role_edges.\\n- `roleGraph map[string]roleGraphEdgesTable` (line 275): the adjacency list of the role inheritance graph.\\n- `LoadRoleGraph` (line 541): populates `roleGraph` from mysql.role_edges.\\n- `FindRole` (line 340): checks if a direct edge exists between a user and role.\\n- `FindAllRole` (line 315): BFS traversal of `roleGraph` to expand all transitively reachable roles from a set of active roles.\\n- `FindAllUserEffectiveRoles` (line 304): filters `activeRoles` against granted roles for the user, then calls `FindAllRole` to do full BFS expansion — this is the core role graph resolution used before every privilege check.\\n- `RequestVerification` (line 1333): calls `FindAllUserEffectiveRoles` to get the full role list, then checks user-level, db-level, table-level, and column-level privileges in order, OR-ing the privilege bitmask across all roles.\\n- `RequestDynamicVerification` (line 1311): calls `HasExplicitlyGrantedDynamicPrivilege`, then falls back to SUPER if SEM permits.\\n- `HasExplicitlyGrantedDynamicPrivilege` (line 1287): checks mysql.global_grants for the dynamic privilege, looping over all effective roles.\\n\\n## SQL Statement → Required Privileges Mapping\\n\\n`pkg/planner/core/planbuilder.go` defines the `visitInfo` struct (line 81) — the data structure recording what privilege is required for which db/table/column. Functions `appendVisitInfo` and `appendDynamicVisitInfo` (defined in `pkg/planner/core/logical_plan_builder.go`) populate the builder's `visitInfo` slice as each SQL clause is processed. `planbuilder.go` contains the main `Build` method dispatch and handles DDL statements (CREATE/DROP/ALTER TABLE, GRANT, REVOKE, SHOW, ADMIN, SET, KILL, etc.), mapping each to specific `mysql.XxxPriv` constants or dynamic privilege names. For example: SHOW CREATE TABLE → ShowViewPriv; SHOW PROCESSLIST → ProcessPriv; SET GLOBAL → SYSTEM_VARIABLES_ADMIN dynamic; KILL → CONNECTION_ADMIN dynamic; GRANT/REVOKE → GrantPriv + SuperPriv or dynamic.\\n\\n`pkg/planner/core/logical_plan_builder.go` handles DML: SELECT → SelectPriv, INSERT → InsertPriv, UPDATE → UpdatePriv, DELETE → DeletePriv. It also checks view definer privileges via `RequestVerificationWithUser` (line 5016) to enforce SQL SECURITY DEFINER semantics.\\n\\n## CheckPrivilege and Its Callers\\n\\n`pkg/planner/core/optimizer.go` defines `CheckPrivilege(activeRoles, pm, vs []visitInfo)` (line 126) — the function that iterates the visitInfo slice and calls `pm.RequestDynamicVerification` for ExtendedPriv entries or `pm.RequestVerification` for all others. `VisitInfo4PrivCheck` (line 155) post-processes visitInfo to handle local temporary table privilege semantics.\\n\\nCallers:\\n- `pkg/planner/optimize.go` (line 501): calls `GetPrivilegeManager` + `VisitInfo4PrivCheck` + `CheckPrivilege` after the logical plan is built.\\n- `pkg/planner/core/plan_cache.go` `checkPreparedPriv` (line 327): re-checks privileges on each execution of a prepared statement.\\n- `pkg/planner/core/preprocess.go` (line 513): calls `RequestVerification` directly during AST pre-processing for database visibility.\\n- `pkg/planner/core/point_get_plan.go` (line 1499): calls `RequestVerification` directly for PointGet fast path.\\n- `pkg/planner/core/expression_codec_fn.go` (line 91): calls `checker.RequestVerification` via the `expropt.PrivilegeChecker` interface for the TIDB_DECODE_TABLE_KEY built-in function.\\n\\n## PrivilegeChecker Interface\\n\\n`pkg/expression/expropt/priv.go` defines the `PrivilegeChecker` interface (a narrower interface with just `RequestVerification`) used by built-in expression functions that need privilege checks without a full session context dependency.\\n\\n## Auth / Connection Layer\\n\\n`pkg/privilege/conn/conn.go` defines `AuthConn`, the interface used by auth plugins (LDAP SASL, extension plugins) to exchange additional packets during authentication.\\n\\n`pkg/privilege/privileges/ldap/` implements LDAP authentication backends (SASL and Simple), invoked from `UserPrivileges.ConnectionVerification`.\\n\\n`pkg/privilege/privileges/tidb_auth_token.go` and `pkg/privilege/privileges/errors.go` provide JWT token auth support and privilege-related error definitions respectively.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
